    <div class="js-template-suggestion px-3 mt-3 hide-sm hide-md d-none" data-template-suggestion-pattern="^FUNDING\.yml$">
      <div data-view-component="true" class="flash">
  
  
        <p>
          <code>.github/FUNDING.yml</code> shows the community how to support this project.

          Please see our
          <a href="https://docs.github.com/articles/displaying-a-sponsor-button-in-your-repository">repository funding links documentation</a>
          for more information on formatting and what is and isn't allowed in this file.
        </p>

          <p>
            Please note that funding links are currently <em>disabled</em> on this repository. Visit
            <a href="/parthdhokane007/parthdhokane007/settings">repository settings</a>
            to enable display of your funding links.
          </p>

    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8 1.5c-2.363 0-4 1.69-4 3.75 0 .984.424 1.625.984 2.304l.214.253c.223.264.47.556.673.848.284.411.537.896.621 1.49a.75.75 0 01-1.484.211c-.04-.282-.163-.547-.37-.847a8.695 8.695 0 00-.542-.68c-.084-.1-.173-.205-.268-.32C3.201 7.75 2.5 6.766 2.5 5.25 2.5 2.31 4.863 0 8 0s5.5 2.31 5.5 5.25c0 1.516-.701 2.5-1.328 3.259-.095.115-.184.22-.268.319-.207.245-.383.453-.541.681-.208.3-.33.565-.37.847a.75.75 0 01-1.485-.212c.084-.593.337-1.078.621-1.489.203-.292.45-.584.673-.848.075-.088.147-.173.213-.253.561-.679.985-1.32.985-2.304 0-2.06-1.637-3.75-4-3.75zM6 15.25a.75.75 0 01.75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 010 1.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 01-.75-.75zM5.75 12a.75.75 0 000 1.5h4.5a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-4.5z"></path>
</svg>
      <strong>ProTip!</strong> Great commit summaries contain fewer than 50 characters. Place extra information in the extended description.
    </div>
